Important News Two

###孔荷寵股竄擾奉高

譚胡各部圍剿孔匪

東固匪巢指日可下

蔣光鼐部在雩剿匪

Nanchang Dispatch: The Red bandit Kong Hechong's band, after being defeated in Pingliu, retreated to Xiushui Tonggu. They repeatedly attempted to invade Nanxun via Yifeng and Wanzai. However, due to the strict defenses of Commander Tan's troops in Tongwan and Commander Liu's brigade in Yifeng, the bandits were unsuccessful. Until the 14th of this month, Kong led over a thousand bandits, with 400 rifles, into Yifeng. They were again met with a fierce attack by Commander Liu's brigade. Kong then secretly fled into the borders of Fengxin and Gao'an counties in Jiangxi. Gao'an and Fengxin are located just over 100 miles from the provincial capital. Now that the bandits have penetrated so deeply, it's like they've thrown themselves into a trap. Therefore, after receiving reports from the magistrates of Gao'an and Fengxin, the headquarters immediately ordered parts of Commanders Tan Daoyuan and Hu Zuyu's divisions, as well as the independent brigade led by Liu Yi, to encircle Kong's bandits in Gao'an and Fengxin. At the same time, strong units were dispatched from the provincial capital to advance towards Fengxin in order to intercept them. It is believed that the bandits will be unable to escape.

Donggu, located at the intersection of Ji'an, Jishui, Yongfeng, and Xingguo, is a major bandit stronghold. Peng Dehuai's band has been trapped there for a long time. Currently, Commander Gong Bingfan's division is attacking the bandit nest in three routes, connecting with Commander Tang's forces. Regarding the Fifth Route Army's Hao Mengling and Guo Huazong's units, on the 15th, they breached the Red bandit fortifications at Tantou, killing several hundred bandits and finally occupying the area. The Red bandits at Wuhua Mountain and Tuolong Pit were also defeated. The remnants of the bandits retreated into Longgang in Donggu. The key passes near Donggu were thus taken by Commanders Gong, Hao, Guo, and Tang. It is reported that Peng's bandits are now extremely panicked, and Donggu will be captured soon. Once Donggu falls, Ningdu will be even easier to pacify.

The three counties of Ningdu, Ruijin, and Shicheng are still occupied by Zhu and Mao. Zhu's bandits are mainly in the area of Dongshao Xiaobu Luokou. However, due to the fierce attacks by government troops, the flags of the fake Soviet governments in various villages have been rolled up and hidden, unlike before when they were displayed proudly. Many fake committee members are hiding in the mountains. Zeng Shan, the fake chairman of the provincial Soviet, issued an urgent notice due to the depletion of food supplies and funds: (1) All public and private property and grain must be handed over by the fake county governments to the fake provincial government for use; (2) All families must provide meals to the Red Army; (3) Each village must recruit 30 able-bodied men to form a guerrilla team to use a circling tactic to harass the rear of the government troops. After receiving this notice, the farmers in various places, unable to resist, fled in large numbers.

Since the Nineteenth Route Army under Jiang Guangnai recaptured the county seat of Yudu, it has been garrisoned by the local police force. The Nineteenth Route Army is currently advancing forward. Unexpectedly, Yudu was recently captured again by small bands of Red bandits. County Magistrate Wang Jingming fled to a neighboring county. Later, large forces arrived to provide assistance, and the bandits retreated. County Magistrate Wang has now returned to the city to handle the aftermath. (May 17th)

Fu Shuangying Discusses the Situation of the Jingxing Mine 63

Daily Coal Production is Two Thousand Tons, Still Seeking Ways to Increase

Annual Revenue from By-Products Approximately Three Million Yuan

Tianjin Dispatch: Fu Shuangying, Director of the Jingxing Mining Bureau, recently visited the mine accompanied by Secretary Su Changgeng. He arrived in Tianjin a few days ago. According to Fu's account of the mine's situation: "The Bureau's various operations are all located at the mine. The mine's equipment is relatively complete, but there are many things that urgently need improvement. I have already appointed De Maotang as the Chief Auditor. This gentleman is of German nationality, but he is treated as a Chinese employee. He is also quite familiar with mining affairs. The mine is about twenty li from the Zhengtai Railway and has its own light railway. It has ten self-owned locomotives and over a hundred coal cars, transporting coal fifty times a day. We have added two more locomotives, which will be transported and installed soon. After that, we can transport coal fifty-seven to sixty times per day. Yesterday, I convened a bureau affairs meeting and decided on the following: 1. Save expenses. State-run enterprises in our country often employ too many people and have high expenses, surpassing those of commercial enterprises. After taking office, I have been determined to open up new revenue streams and reduce expenditures. I will evaluate employees, dismiss those who have nothing to do, replace those who are incompetent, and add assistants to those who are busy. 2. Increase production. The mine produces more than 2,000 tons of coal per day, but half of the workers are local farmers. Now, during the busy farming season, they have all resigned to return home to farm, resulting in a decrease in production. We have decided to hire workers from other places, hoping to achieve a daily coal production target of more than 3,000 tons in the near future. We will continue to find ways to gradually increase production in the future. 3. Increase transportation capacity. To develop the business, the first priority is to facilitate transportation. The biggest difficulty for the mine is the lack of vehicles. Only a few tens of thousands of tons of coal were transported to Tianjin last month, which was far from meeting demand. Currently, only three trains have been allocated by the Beining Railway and only two trains by the Pinghan Railway. We are negotiating with the Pinghan Railway to allocate two more trains, which is expected to be achieved. 4. Increase by-products. The mine's coal is the main product, but by-products are also important. What are by-products? They are the coke oven plant. Coke is made from bituminous coal, which is well known, but the various types of oils produced by the coke oven plant may not be clear to the general public. Here is a brief description: (1) The coal tar distillation unit produces nine types of products, including asphalt oil, red oil, and black paint. (2) The xylene oil distillation unit produces motor oil and crude xylene oil. (3) The fertilizer manufacturing unit produces finished products from sulfuric acid solution and sulfuric acid. The revenue from these by-products is no less than three million yuan per year, which is about the same as the revenue from coal sales. And the profit from these by-products is better than that of the main product, so we are increasing coal production and expanding the coke oven. (May 17th)

Shenhai Railway Expands Towards the Chaofu Branch Line 64

And Takes Over the Jinggou Coal Mine

Shenyang Dispatch: The Shenhai Railway Company is a joint public-private venture with a capital of 20 million yuan. In 1927, the main line was opened to traffic. Subsequently, the Meixi branch line was built. By 1930, the business gradually developed. It is now actively expanding the Chaofu branch line. The estimated construction cost for the Chaohui and Huixing sections is over 2.11 million yuan. Subsidiary businesses are also being actively expanded. For example, the Jinggou Coal Mine Company, which was jointly operated by the company and the business community, has been taken over for self-management. The company held its fourth shareholders' meeting on the 15th of this month and re-elected commercial shareholder associates and supervisors. Director-General Zhang Huilin reported on the business overview and work progress of 1930, as well as the work plan for 1931. Details of the Chaofu branch line, Jinggou Coal Mine, and business overview of 1930 are recorded below:

Expanding the Chaofu Branch Line: Huinan, Mengjiang, Fusong, and other counties east of Chaoyang Town, the terminus of the Shenhai Railway, are densely populated with forests and mines, and the land is fertile. They are renowned and prosperous regions in the Northeast. However, the mountains are layered and the transportation is inconvenient, so useful materials cannot be exported. The railway company therefore plans to build the Chaofu branch line to break the blockade and unlock treasures. In March of last year, the company sent Ouyang Ling, the former chief of the engineering section, to organize a survey team to survey the route from Chaoyang Town to Mengjiang, a distance of 90 kilometers. Except for the Chaohui section, which still uses the route surveyed in the winter of 1928 on the Chaoshan line, there are three lines surveyed for the Huimeng section: one from Huinan via Pubanshi and Sipenling to Mengjiang, one from Huinan via Shansonggang and Jinchuan County to Mengjiang, and one from Huinan via Xinkailing, Xinglongbao, and Sichaling to Mengjiang. The above three lines all have difficulties, such as excessively long tunnels, excessively steep slopes, or excessively long routes, and a decision could not be made at the time. Later, in early November, the associate director of the railway and the chief of the engineering department, along with Liao, the section chief of the Northeast Transportation Committee, personally surveyed the Huimeng section of the route. They all agreed that the line via Xinkailing, Xinglongbao, and Sichaling was the most suitable. It was immediately decided to adopt this line, and a budget for the construction costs of the Chaohui and Huixing sections of the Chaofu branch line was drafted and submitted to the provincial government and the Transportation Committee for review and approval. Construction will begin as soon as approval is granted. Budget for the construction costs of the Chaohui and Huixing sections of the Chaofu branch line: The total length of the two sections is 49 kilometers, with four stations, eight kilometers of sidings, and three kilometers of gravel lines, for a total cost of 2,119,900 yuan (excluding vehicles).

Taking Over the Jinggou Coal Mine: The Jinchao Coal Mine Company was originally jointly operated by the Shenhai Railway Company and businessman Zhou Wenfu. In July 1930, Zhou Wenfu, the general manager of the mine company, stated that the mine's business was difficult to develop due to the joint public-private partnership. He requested to withdraw commercial shares and return to public self-management, and was willing to value the mine's production machinery, etc. at 200,000 yuan, which would be exchanged for the railway company's stock. The railway company considered that the change of jointly operated mining was a major issue, and the decision was made after the 16th board of directors and supervisors meeting, and the approval of the provincial government was obtained to take it back for self-management with a valuation of 200,000 yuan in cash, which was offset by 6,000 shares. The railway company then sent personnel to take over the mine and named it the Jinggou Coal Mine of the Shenhai Railway Company, and appointed former manager Zhou Wenying as the mine director to manage its affairs. Subsequently, a letter was sent to the Finance and Agriculture and Mining Departments to send personnel to assist in estimating the exact amount of the mine's assets. The total amount of assets was estimated to be 695,835.363 yuan, and after deducting debts of 380,569.09 yuan, the total amount of actual assets was 315,666.273 yuan. The mine is currently actively planning to develop.

Summary of Last Year's Operations: The total revenue of the Shenhai Railway Company in 1930 was 7,623,039.16 yuan, an increase of 2,279,953 yuan compared to last year. The total expenditure for operations was 4,321,450.097 yuan, leaving a net surplus of 3,301,588.19 yuan. After deducting dividends, interest, and unpaid military transport fees of 1,743,974.15 yuan, the total net profit was 1,557,614.04 yuan. (May 15th)

Zhenjiang Dispatch: The Jiangsu Provincial Higher Qualification Examination continued yesterday. In the first session in the morning, committee members Ma Yinchu, Hu Dunfu, and Yu Qingtang presided over the examination. Ninety-nine candidates took the test, which began at 7:30 AM. The subjects tested were economics, advanced mathematics, mathematics, and educational administration. All papers were submitted before 10:00 AM. In the second session, only one candidate took the foreign language test. In the first session in the afternoon, committee member Liu Yimou presided over the Chinese and foreign history test. In the second session, committee member Xie Guansheng presided over the administrative law and civil law test. The order was very solemn. It is reported that yesterday's test papers have been partially reviewed by the chief examiners and assistant examiners. After the review is completed, the office staff will unseal and score the papers separately. It is expected that the results will be announced tomorrow. It is also reported that the qualification examination certificates should have been announced by the Examination Yuan, and unified measures should have been formulated by the central government. However, the certificates have not yet been issued. Yesterday, Commissioner Su specially sent a telegram urging them to expedite the review and approval and issue them. (May 19th)

Harbin Merchants Oppose the Special Monopoly on Matches in Eastern Provinces 66

Telegram Urges Northeast Authorities to Abolish the Special Bureau

Harbin Dispatch: The Eastern Provinces' implementation of a special sales tax on matches, with the addition of stamps, is about to begin. The two chambers of commerce in Harbin believe that in the midst of this nationwide abolition of likin, the sudden establishment of a match monopoly bureau and the imposition of heavy taxes will increase the burden on the people, which contradicts the government's intention to abolish likin and alleviate difficulties. Therefore, a meeting was held at the Binjiang Municipal Chamber of Commerce last night to discuss the matter. As a result of the discussion, it was unanimously decided to send a telegram to the authorities, requesting the abolition of the special bureau. The original text is as follows: The National Government has legally abolished likin nationwide. The highest authorities in the Northeast have strictly ordered all provinces in the Northeast to follow the National Government's order to abolish likin and not to increase or levy new taxes under any pretext. On April 3 of this year, the National Government also issued an explicit order to abolish the plan to implement special consumption taxes after the abolition of likin. Fearing that the provinces would not implement it effectively, the order was reiterated on the same day, stating: "The abolition of likin and all taxes similar to likin is a national policy. The competent ministry has followed the order to issue a circular to implement it as scheduled. If provincial governments are still disobeying previous orders to abolish likin or are creating new names and arbitrarily collecting taxes similar to likin, the Control Yuan should be responsible for sending personnel to conduct on-site investigations and reporting for punishment, in order to emphasize official orders and discipline." This order shows the central government's and your Excellency's determination to love and protect our people and resolutely abolish likin. However, unexpectedly, the Northeast Match Association has been approved to establish a match monopoly bureau and levy heavy taxes, with each small box of one hundred matches being affixed with a special monopoly stamp worth two cents. This is equivalent to levying more than 20% of the original price. Even previous likin taxes were not this heavy. The establishment of match monopoly bureaus by various provinces contradicts the cotton yarn, match, and cement unified tax regulations formulated by the National Government and is illegal and should not be established. Moreover, the imposition of excessive taxes is even more inappropriate. May we ask, what is the purpose of establishing a bureau to monopolize the sale of matches and affix heavy taxes on stamps? If it is to increase revenue, it violates the laws and regulations on the abolition of likin. If it is intended to resist foreign matches and protect domestic industries, the National Government has long established the Dumping Tax Law, which can be implemented by following it. There is no need to establish a separate monopoly agency, adding to the waste of resources. Protecting domestic industries should be tax-free. We have never heard of increasing taxes on domestic goods and calling it protection. Matches, although a necessity for all, even the poor, their value is related to people's livelihood. Selling matches and collecting heavy taxes is harmful to people's livelihood. We respectfully request that you examine and verify this matter and order the abolition of the Northeast Match Monopoly measures to comply with laws and benefit the people. Please reply by telegram after processing. Harbin Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Jilin Binjiang Municipal Chamber of Commerce, bowing together. (May 12th)

Disputes Over the Collection of Boat Tax on the Changhuai River 67

The Water Police Bureau Awaits Orders to Hand Over

The Ship Management Office is About to Begin Collection

Bengbu Dispatch: The Anhui Provincial Government has established a provincial ship management office. All ships in the province's Yangtze River basin, Changhuai River basin, and within Chaohu Lake must be charged license fees and registration fees in accordance with the management regulations decided by the provincial government committee. Even foreign small steamers must be charged temporary transit permit fees. In northern Anhui, the first to be affected is the Changhuai River Water Police Bureau. The salaries and expenses of the bureau's director and police rely entirely on the Changhuai River boat tax. The monthly recurring expenses amount to over 9,000 yuan. The eight boat tax offices established collect 5,000 yuan per month. In addition, the provincial government subsidizes 4,000 yuan per month, so the bureau has been able to maintain its current state in recent years. Now that the Provincial Ship Management Office has been established, the Changhuai River boat tax will of course be collected by the office. Once implemented, the Changhuai River Water Police Bureau will be cut off from its lifeline, and water security will inevitably be greatly affected. The bureau's director, Lu Fengshu, recently reported this situation to the provincial government and requested instructions on how to proceed. A telegram was received stating that half of the bureau's police expenses for 1930 would be allocated monthly by the Ship Management Office. The remaining amount would still be allocated by the provincial government. Starting from July 1931, the bureau's expenses would be fully paid by the provincial government on a monthly basis. However, based on past experience, the provincial government's subsidies to the bureau have not always been allocated monthly, sometimes being delayed for four or five months. It remains to be seen whether they can be allocated monthly in the future and whether the bureau's police expenses will face difficulties. According to Director Lu of the bureau, the bureau has decided to hand over the Changhuai River boat tax to the Ship Management Office for collection. Once the provincial government's telegram order is received, it will be handed over for collection by the office. It is reported that the Ministry of Communications believes that the Anhui Provincial Ship Management Office's regulations for managing small steamers are too strict, with high fees for license renewals, which conflicts with the Ship Registration Law promulgated by the National Government last year. The Anhui Provincial Government has been consulted and instructed to stop implementation or to revise the regulations to alleviate the merchants' difficulties. However, the authorities are determined to implement it, and it is unknown whether they will accept it. (May 18th)

Hangzhou Quick Mail 68

Cooperative enterprises are related to the farmers' economy. The Department of Construction has been actively promoting them and has sent personnel to various counties and towns in eastern and western Zhejiang to vigorously publicize and guide them. The entire province has also been divided into eight districts to allocate work.

Most of the cocoon firms in various towns have suspended operations due to the impact of the financial crisis this year. Although the Department of Construction is trying its best to help farmers sell cocoons and has formulated relief measures, ordering various counties to follow them, the cocoon merchants have taken a passive attitude. Even those that have opened have mostly merged operations to save expenses. The cocoon situation is unprecedented.

The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau, due to the expansion of routes and the shortage of vehicles, former Director Chen requested the Department of Construction to negotiate with the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank to borrow 30,000 yuan in cash. The case was submitted to the Political Committee for resolution. The current Acting Highway Director Huang has signed a contract to receive the funds and plans to send personnel to Shanghai to order new vehicles as soon as possible for transportation to Hangzhou for distribution to various routes.

The Hangzhou Municipal Chamber of Commerce has sent letters to various trade associations regarding the issue of collecting accounts on three festivals. The Chamber of Commerce had previously decided that the three festivals of Lichun (Start of Spring), Xiazhi (Summer Solstice), and Qiufen (Autumn Equinox) would be the common accounting periods. However, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce decided that in accordance with the solar terms, the end of May, close to Xiaoman (Grain Full), and the end of September, close to Qiufen (Autumn Equinox), would still be the first and second accounting dates, and the day before Lichun each year would be the business community's final accounting period. Now that the summer festival is approaching, opinions are being solicited on how to determine the specific method. (May 19th)

After investigation by the High Court, the accusation was found to be true. Yesterday (19th), President Lin issued an order to dismiss him and await investigation. Police and Bandits Exchange Fire in Guajing: The eighth squad of the second district of the Water Police, under the command of Squad Leader Wang Chuan, departed from Tingzigang on the previous day to search for bandits. While passing Maoqigang, they were informed by local residents that a large gang of bandits was not far away. Squad Leader Wang immediately ordered the first and third squads to encircle and advance on two routes. When they reached Guajing, it was already dusk. Wujiang 70

The Kidnapped Victim in Beidian Escapes Danger: Ni Chengying's family in Zhuangtian Village, attached to Beidian Town in the county, had his mother, Madam Li, his younger brother, Qi Guan, and a maid, A Jin, kidnapped by bandits last month. This case has been reported in previous newspapers. After Madam Li escaped from the bandit den, she hired someone to contact the bandits and negotiated a ransom of 2,200 yuan. After the ransom was paid, the bandits suddenly released the maid, A Jin, but demanded 50,000 yuan for Qi Guan. Later, Ni's family contacted and negotiated with the bandits and sent another 500 yuan. The bandits finally agreed to release Qi Guan, who safely arrived home yesterday.

The Affair of a Construction Bureau Official: Zhang Langyao, a relative of the Construction Bureau Chief Tang Shizhen, who currently serves as the bureau's accountant, has recently fallen in love with Pang Shoulong's daughter, Jinbao, from Shengtangqiao in the city. His wife, Madam Yin, found out about the affair. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, she led servants to Pang's house to catch them in the act. Zhang was chatting with Jinbao. Suddenly hearing that his wife was coming, he climbed onto the roof to escape, but inadvertently fell into the neighbor Gu Ziyuan's garden. The garden owner was away and the gate was tightly closed, so Zhang could not get out, causing a sensation throughout the city.

Wuxi 71

Cocoon Industry Association Resolves Important Cases: The Wuxi Cocoon Industry Association held a special executive committee meeting yesterday to discuss the many urgent matters that need to be discussed by the industry as new cocoons are about to be on the market. The following are the resolutions of the important cases: (1) The issue of cocoon firms paying business tax. Wuxi has not collected business tax from various industries, and cocoon firms have already paid the brokerage tax. It should be replied to the Chamber of Commerce and forwarded to the Finance Department to request exemption from collection. (2) This year's cocoon season is poor, and the business of cocoon firms will inevitably be reduced. All firms are adopting a tight policy and reducing all expenses. Only temporary employees with employment letters will be hired, and others will not be accepted. (3) It was decided to convene a spring industry conference on the 27th of this month.

Decision to Widen the West City Foot Standard: The Wuxi County Government held its 92nd county administration meeting yesterday and resolved the following important cases: (1) The widening of West City Foot Street was decided to be handled in accordance with the widening width of Lu Hua Lane. (2) The section of the street where the Xicheng Road and Tonghui Road meet should be handled in accordance with Tonghui Road. As for the Xin surname and other properties, they will be postponed due to the county's financial constraints. (3) The 600 yuan estimated cost of printing resident permits should be included in the 1931 county local budget expenses for payment. (4) The case of Zhao Hongbin, the district chief of the 7th district, requesting to install a 10% reserve fund for township telephones and telephone equipment, and planning to use the existing coupons, was decided that for trunk lines, if the amount is not an integer, it can be borrowed from the existing coupons. However, for branch lines, the request for borrowing should not be supported.

Ding Shuangsheng's Shopkeeper Apprehended by the Court: Ding Xingchu and Ding Hesheng, brothers and owners of the Ding Shuangsheng silk shop on Dashiqiao in the city, failed in speculative ventures and owed more than 200,000 yuan. The creditors requested the County Chamber of Commerce to clear them up, inventory and seal the property and goods, and publish advertisements for bids. Unexpectedly, another part of the creditors filed a lawsuit in the judiciary, which has not been resolved for two months. Yesterday, Qin Yiji and others, the creditors, learned that Ding Xingchu was at lawyer Xue Naichuan's house on the embankment, secretly discussing ways to deal with the lawsuit. They notified the creditors, waited for Ding Xingchu to come out, and went forward to arrest him. They were handed over to the first branch of the Public Security Bureau, which transferred them to the General Bureau. Since the matter was a monetary dispute, they were transferred to the County Court, where Prosecutor Du of the Prosecutor's Office opened a court for interrogation. At that time, a total of eighty-nine men and women from the creditor side arrived, and Qin Yiji, Sun Yiji, Bao Juji, Xu Yiji, Ni Guanji and other five households were selected as representatives. As a result of the interrogation, Ding Xingchu was ordered to be detained. If he wanted to be released on bail, he had to pay 200,000 yuan in cash. The creditors were also ordered to return.

Rice Prices Soar in Wuxi: In the past month, Wuxi has been experiencing continuous rain, and wheat has become hopeless. Therefore, japonica and indica rice have been continuously soaring in price. Various counties have also come to Wuxi to purchase them. Some unscrupulous merchants are also taking the opportunity to smuggle rice and rice stocks overseas. The bottom is drying up day by day, and the source is also small. Therefore, rice prices have been soaring in recent days, rising by more than two yuan per picul. The current market price of high-quality white rice is already 11.7 yuan, and the future of the people's food is very worrying.

Verdict on the Case of Suffocating His Wife to Death: Huang Rongchu, a villager from Cheng Tangxiang, Tianshang City, Sixth District, suffocated his wife, Shen Qinxian, to death. The case has been investigated and concluded by the Court Prosecutor's Office, and a public prosecution has been initiated. It is now known that yesterday was the date for the verdict of this case. At 10:00 AM, Court President and Judge Yang Keqian took the seat in the first court, proposed the Huang Rongchu proposal, announced the verdict's main text, and sentenced him to twelve years of imprisonment. After the verdict, he was sent to prison for execution.

Rampant Banditry in Siyang and Suqian: The Pacification Superintendent's Office received a telegraphic report from Chen Yingcai, the District Chief of the Third District of Siyang, and others, stating that in recent days, on the border between Siyang and Suqian, communist bandits were discovered distributing leaflets and colluding with local bandits led by Wei Yousan. Nantong 74

Extremely Prosperous Coastal Fishing in Northern Jiangsu: Fishing households in Lusi, Juegang, Fengli, and other areas along the coast of northern Jiangsu Province are exporting fishing boats one after another because the sea bandits in the ocean have been eliminated. In recent days, the yellow croaker and pomfret fishing season is in full swing, and the fishing households are returning fully loaded. This good omen, it is said, has not been seen for four or five years.

Three Counties Jointly Manage the Protection of Sandbar Collapse: Xu Ji, commissioned by the Department of Construction, convened county magistrates, directors of construction bureaus, and representatives from all walks of life from Nantong, Changshu, and Jiangyin on the 18th at Liuhai Sandbar to discuss the joint management of sandbar and riverbank protection against collapse by the three counties.

Gaoyou 75

Grain Boat Sinks in Gaoyou Lake: Chen Zhongfu, a grain merchant from Suqian, previously loaded a boat with miscellaneous grains in that county, preparing to sell them in Shaobo. Huzhou 76

Military Police Search and Suppress Bandits, Rescue Hostages: Banditry in the western countryside of Huzhou is becoming increasingly rampant. Kidnappings and intimidation are heard of every day. Now is the time when silkworm cocoons are being marketed, so the local military police in various places are searching everywhere to prevent bandit troubles. The day before yesterday (the 16th) at around 6 a.m., the Third Battalion of the Security Team stationed in Si sent many soldiers from the battalion headquarters to Lincheng Bridge on the Xintong'an steamer to dock. The soldiers disembarked and went to the Wunicao area, where they saw a group of bandits. The troops immediately opened fire, and the bandits returned fire to resist arrest. The two sides fought for about half an hour before the bandits were defeated and fled. One bandit was captured on the spot, one was killed, and one Mauser pistol was seized. The captured bandit was taken to the headquarters for interrogation. The 11th Marine Police Team learned that several bandits, along with two hostages, were hiding in the home of a resident surnamed Wu near Dawu Mountain a few days ago. The team immediately dispatched more than 30 marine patrolmen to the area to suppress and arrest them. Unexpectedly, the bandits had already fled upon hearing the news. The two hostages were rescued from danger. It is reported that one hostage was the owner of a rice shop in Changxing, and the other was the son of a farmer from Nanqiao. The team has already notified their families to claim them. Furthermore, the Fourth Company of the Security Team was patrolling near the Heqi Meishan Railway the day before yesterday when they encountered several bandits carrying a hostage. The bandits, upon seeing the troops, abandoned the hostage and fled in all directions. The hostage was taken back, and it was said that he was the son of a Mr. Pan from Lincheng Bridge. Pan has been notified to come and claim him.

Jiashan 77

Farmer Kidnapped by Bandits: The home of Ni Quanfu, a farmer living in Dongchangbang outside the east gate, was suddenly invaded by more than a dozen bandits carrying weapons at around 3 a.m. the night before last. They broke down the door, searched for and looted clothes and other items, and kidnapped Ni Lianqing, who was taken away to the north with shouts. It is now reported that Ni Quanfu has received a letter from the bandits demanding a huge ransom.

Jiaxing 78

Cocoon Industry Conference Opens: The Jiaxing Cocoon Industry Association held a business meeting on the afternoon of the 18th. More than 40 representatives of factories signed in. Zhu Mou first reported on the current state of the world silk market, which is equivalent to 600 taels of silver per dan. Cocoons need to be purchased according to this price standard. The following resolutions were passed: (1) The purchase price of cocoons shall be a maximum of 42 yuan and a minimum of 38 yuan per dan. Each factory shall deposit 100 yuan with the association in advance. If anyone exceeds this amount without authorization, the money will be confiscated and used as membership dues. (2) The opening date for cocoon purchases shall be the 23rd in Jianan and the 24th in Jianbei. If cocoon samples are not seen by then, the date may be postponed by one or two days. (3) Existing local public welfare and educational donations will continue to be handled according to the old plan.

Marine Police Detain Suspects: The Ninth Marine Police Team stationed in Baima Weir recently checked a ship passing through the border and found a net boat coming from Jiaxing with two passengers, Wu Jin'a Da and Wu Fuchang. They had a package containing many clothes and ornaments. When asked about their origin, they were hesitant and evasive, seeming to be suspected bandits. The people and the goods were detained and sent to the Jiaxing County Government for investigation. The county government sent them to the Public Security Bureau for handling. According to Wu Jin'a Da's confession, he is 40 years old, from Pinghu, and has been working as a boatman. He is not a thief. Wu Fuchang confessed that he is 34 years old, from Pinghu, and is currently working as a bricklayer. The County Public Security Bureau, considering that it is a period of clearing the countryside, should thoroughly investigate, so they sent the people and the goods to the County Clearing Bureau for interrogation yesterday.

Hangzhou 79

Collapse of Provincial People's Education Center Injures People: The People's Paradise attached to the Provincial People's Education Center on Hubin Road in Hangzhou's New Market is located upstairs in the center's building. It usually has books and newspapers for the public to relax and enjoy themselves, and also has seats for selling tea. The business is quite prosperous. Recently, due to continuous wind and rain, the northern part of the building above the center suddenly collapsed yesterday afternoon, injuring Ding Yunlin, Wang Zhongyu, Chen Zhongkui, Wang Xiaofa, Xu Jiangquan, and six others. Hu Douwen, the director of the center, sent staff member Wei Yanran to hire a car to take them to the Municipal Hospital for treatment. It is reported that their lives are not in danger.

Ningbo 80

Re-election of Officials of the Lawyers' Association: The Yinxian Lawyers' Association held a supplementary spring general meeting yesterday (the 17th) at 1 p.m. and re-elected officials. Fifty-eight members, including Luo Huang, attended. After discussing the proposals, the election was held. As a result, Huang Rongchang was elected as the president, and Tong Baoheng was elected as the vice president. Luo Huang, Xin Yi, Chen Ji, Song Zeng, Bi Wenbing, Yan Pengling, Zhang Zhenxiao, Mao Yifeng, and eight others were elected as councilors.

Ge Cisheng is Willing to Die to Repay the Bodhisattva: The wooden puppets of the old and new City God Temples in Ningbo have been destroyed by various party and government circles to eliminate superstition for two years. Unexpectedly, recently, a stubborn man named Ge Cisheng secretly made two City God Bodhisattva statues at home. Yesterday morning, he gathered more than a hundred followers and carried them into the old and new City God Temples for worship. The county government ordered the Public Security Bureau to send police to stop them, but they refused to listen. The county party department heard the news and immediately convened representatives from military police and other agencies to hold an emergency meeting. It was decided to send a large team of military police to the temple to disperse the crowd and destroy the puppets. Ge Cisheng, seeing the large team of military police arriving, feigned madness and lay in the hall, claiming that he was willing to die to repay the puppets. He was then carried home by others. It is reported that the county party department believes that Ge's actions are reckless and incite superstition and confuse the public, and will write to the judicial authorities to detain and strictly punish him.

Changsha City Levies Entertainment Tax 82

To Subsidize Primary School Education Funds

Changsha Correspondence on May 15: According to a survey by the Changsha Municipal Preparatory Office, there are approximately 40,000 school-age children in Changsha City, but only more than 23,000 are enrolled. In addition, there are more than 17,000 children who are out of school, all because there are too few primary schools and no place to accommodate them. To increase the number of primary schools or expand the number of classes requires additional funding. Guo Fangrui, director of the Municipal Preparatory Office, petitioned the provincial government to levy an entertainment tax to subsidize it. All cinemas, Beijing-Hankou civilian theaters, and dance halls in Changsha City will be charged 5% of the ticket price, effective from June 1. It is estimated that there are more than a dozen large and small theaters in Changsha, each of which can sell an average of more than 100 yuan worth of tickets per day, which can generate 60 to 70 yuan in tax, resulting in more than 2,000 yuan per month, which will greatly benefit primary school education. The collection regulations are recorded as follows:

Article 1: All those engaged in recreational and entertainment businesses within the city shall comply with the provisions of these simple regulations and levy a surcharge. Article 2: The types of entertainment tax are as follows: (1) Cinemas, (2) Beijing opera theaters, (3) Han opera theaters, (4) Civilian theaters, (5) Dance halls, (6) Large and small amusement parks (temporary park residents and various miscellaneous items without a fixed place are not included in this example). Article 3: The entertainment tax shall be 5% of the ticket value of each venue. If tickets are not used and seats are sold by other methods, this article shall still apply, and the tax shall be levied on the total amount. Article 4: The entertainment tax shall be stamped with an additional chop on the tickets of each entertainment venue, and shall be collected with the tickets at the time of sale, and paid to the competent tax collection office for verification and receipt on a daily basis. However, when necessary, each entertainment venue may submit a request to the tax collection office, which shall forward it to the Municipal Preparatory Office, which shall determine a corresponding tax amount and instruct the operators to pay separately. The method shall be determined separately. Article 5: When necessary, the tax collection office may inspect the account books and ticket stubs of each entertainment venue to collect the entertainment tax. Article 6: Entertainment venues shall not overcharge, underreport, or delay payment of surcharges. Violators shall be punished by the tax collection office, which shall submit a request to the Municipal Preparatory Office. Article 7: In addition to paying taxes in accordance with these simple regulations, each entertainment venue shall also comply with various regulatory procedures promulgated by the government. Article 8: If there are any matters not covered in these simple regulations, the Municipal Preparatory Office shall modify them at any time. Article 9: These simple regulations shall be implemented from the date they are approved by the Hunan Provincial Department of Construction.

Local News

Municipal Education Bureau Announces Examination Regulations for Senior Civil Service Examinations for Agriculture and Forestry Administrative Personnel 84

The Examination Yuan has formulated and announced the implementation of the Examination Regulations for Senior Civil Service Examinations for Agriculture and Forestry Administrative Personnel, and has consulted the Executive Yuan to instruct all its subordinates to be informed. Now, the Municipal Education Bureau has received instructions from the Ministry of Education to issue the regulations and instruct all its subordinates to be informed and comply. The original text of the regulations is as follows:

Article 1 of the Examination Regulations for Senior Civil Service Examinations for Agriculture and Forestry Administrative Personnel: Unless otherwise provided by law, the senior examinations for agriculture and forestry administrative personnel shall be conducted in accordance with the provisions of these regulations. Article 2: Citizens of the Republic of China who have one of the following qualifications may take the senior examinations for agriculture and forestry administrative personnel: (1) Graduates from national or registered public or private universities, independent colleges, or vocational schools who have studied agriculture and forestry subjects for more than three years and have obtained a certificate; (2) Graduates from foreign universities, independent colleges, or vocational schools recognized by the Ministry of Education who have studied agriculture and forestry subjects for more than three years and have obtained a certificate; (3) Those who have the same academic ability as graduates of agriculture and forestry departments of universities or vocational schools and have passed the qualification examination; (4) Those who have confirmed professional knowledge, experience, or writings in forestry that have passed the review; (5) Those who have passed the ordinary examination for agricultural and forestry technicians and have served in agricultural agencies for more than four years or have held a commissioned official position or a position equivalent to a commissioned official for more than three years. Article 3: The subjects of the first examination are as follows: Chinese: 1. Essay, 2. Official Documents; Party Principles: 1. Three Principles of the People, 2. Outline of National Reconstruction, 3. Strategies for National Reconstruction, 4. Important Declarations and Resolutions of the Chinese Nationalist Party. Article 4: The subjects of the second examination are as follows: (1) Agricultural Administration Department: Required Subjects: 1. Organization Law of the National Government, 2. Introduction to Jurisprudence, 3. Rural Sociology, 4. General Agriculture, 5. Agricultural Economics, 6. Agricultural Policy, 7. Forestry Policy, 8. Agricultural Laws and Regulations; Elective Subjects: 1. Rural Autonomy, 2. Rural Education, 3. Rural Cooperation, 4. Agricultural Finance, 5. Agricultural Management, 6. Agricultural History, 7. Agricultural Geography, 8. Agricultural Statistics, 9. Agricultural Extension; Select three of the above elective subjects. (2) Forestry Administration Department: Required Subjects: 1. Organization Law of the National Government, 2. Introduction to Jurisprudence, 3. Forest Police Science, 4. Forestry Economics, 5. Forestry Policy, 6. Forestry Laws and Regulations, 7. Forestry Management; Elective Subjects: 1. Meilin Botany, 2. Forest Protection Science, 3. Afforestation Science, 4. Forest Utilization Science; Select two of the above elective subjects. Article 5: The third examination shall be based on the examinee's written examination subjects and experience interview. Article 6: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Results of the Secondary School Curriculum Standard Experiment at Shanghai Municipal Wuben Girls' High School 86

Since last year, Shanghai Municipal Wuben Girls' High School has organized a teaching staff secondary school curriculum standard research association. Based on the teaching experience of colleagues, regular meetings are held every month to objectively, scientifically, and carefully discuss and analyze the current secondary school textbooks and the teaching material outlines stipulated by the curriculum standards, compare their advantages and disadvantages, and then apply them to practice according to the stipulated teaching methods. The results of the experiment are divided into five major categories and reported as follows:

Regarding the objectives of each subject: 1. The objective of high school mathematics seems to be to add the habit of cultivating students' calm and quiet solution of difficult problems, so that they can face difficulties without fear and not be discouraged by failure. (Reason) In addition to striving for practicality, high school students should cultivate the courage to struggle and the spirit of solving difficult problems, so that they can pursue advanced academic studies or strive to serve the community.

Regarding the key points of each subject assignment: (1) In the high school English assignment key points column, the coordination of the procedures for ear, mouth, eye, and hand training is good, but high school English should pay special attention to eye and hand exercises. (Reason) High school English courses should focus more on the ability to read and write, so eye and hand exercises are more important than ear and mouth training. (2) In the high school mathematics assignment, actual application triangles should be added to measure nearby schools and other places. (Reason) Surveying is one of the construction works in the period of political training, which directly applies triangles. Therefore, when learning triangles, paying attention to surveying is directly promoting the application of theory to practice and indirectly cultivating the skills to engage in occupations.

Regarding the time allocation of each subject: 1. The intensive reading guidance time for junior high school Chinese should be increased to four hours. (Reason) According to the results of the experiment, the selected texts for intensive reading are relatively long and complex, and each unit cannot be completed within three hours. Shorter ones are slightly longer than three hours. If one hour can be added, the longer and more complex ones can be completed in one unit each week, and the shorter and simpler ones can be taught in two consecutive lessons, which can also come to an end within each week. 2. High school Chinese composition should be done by students outside of class. (Reason) High school students' composition focuses on thematic research and attempts at literary works, both of which require more than two hours of time. According to the results of the experiment, the time is directly proportional to the score. The scores of those who write in class are inferior to those who write outside of class. If the deadline for submission is limited and attention is paid to eliminating plagiarism and other malpractices, not only can students be allowed to create calmly and organize better articles, but also the composition time can be moved to other needs. 3. The time allocation of junior high school arithmetic should be changed to five hours of arithmetic in the first grade's upper and lower semesters, five hours of algebra in the second grade's lower semester, and five hours of geometry in the third grade's upper and lower semesters, plus a three-hour optional course in trigonometry. (

semester five hours of arithmetic, lower semester two hours of arithmetic, three hours of algebra, but in terms of arithmetic material, it must be connected with elementary school arithmetic and expanded, especially inserting application exercises related to the knowledge and experience of daily life, such as abacus and other materials are so many, students' level is shorter by one year in elementary school, and it is even different from the past, so there is an impact on the progress. According to the actual teaching experience, the first semester of junior high school is changed to five hours of arithmetic, and the basic concepts of algebra, positive and negative numbers, and simple equations are used to estimate a way to introduce algebra while teaching arithmetic, and the foundation is considered to be more solid, without the malpractice of being half-baked and mixed but not specialized. Then, when studying algebra geometry in the second and third grades, it seems that the obstruction of unclear concepts and unclear analysis can be avoided. As for the selection of materials in the trigonometry part, it seems that practical measurement should be the main focus, and a three-hour elective course should be set in the lower semester of the third grade to teach it, so that students who go on to school and find employment can get the best of both worlds. 4. High school mathematics, according to the general table, has 19 credits, and according to the sub-table, there are only 18 credits, so it is known that there must be a mistake in the middle, but according to the results of the three-semester experiment of the affiliated school, the total time is always insufficient, and it is not easy to complete the teaching material outline in the curriculum standard as scheduled. It is set to be 20 credits, adding one credit to trigonometry in the fourth semester and subtracting one credit from analytic geometry, and changing analytic geometry to four credits in the fifth semester. 5. The original time allocation for junior high school botany and zoology was set at three credits each, and the teaching materials and teaching methods were tested according to the prescribed teaching material outline and teaching methods. It is always felt that the time is far from enough. If you want to reduce the teaching materials to fit the time, then all the teaching materials set are very appropriate and cannot be abandoned. Therefore, according to the results of the experiment, at least one credit should be added to each, for a total of eight credits.

Regarding the teaching material outline of each subject: 1. The amount of classical Chinese in the teaching materials of junior high school Chinese should be slightly increased in each academic year. (Reason) According to students' learning status, the perception of classical Chinese selected texts seems to be deeper. In terms of recitation, classical Chinese is especially easy to achieve results, and junior high school is the foundation for cultivating students' classical Chinese skills. If the classical Chinese teaching materials can be reduced without being too much, the opportunity to be trained will be easier to obtain. 2. The high school English teaching material outline is still rich in content, but the grammar of ordinary English in the first and second grades of high school should be included. (Reason) The third grade of high school has rhetoric essentials. If grammar is not taught separately in the first and second grades, the foundation of sentence construction and composition is not solid, and the rhetoric essentials of the third grade are difficult to learn. 3. High school mathematics teaching material outline, regarding the equation group of algebra, the ordinary theorem and application of determinants should be added under item (B). (Reason) Determinants are the general method for solving general linear equations, and they must be applied in analytic geometry, and they are widely used, so they should be taught. Also, regarding geometry, the quadratic curve in item (D) should be deleted and included in analytic geometry. (Reason) It is not easy to understand when teaching quadratic curves in Euclidean geometry, and it takes time. It is quite suitable to teach in analytic geometry. Otherwise, if quadratic curves are taught immediately after solid geometry, not only will the mind be unclear, but it will also be redundant in analytic geometry. 4. High school and junior high school national history and foreign history teaching material outline: A. There are too many political historical materials. (Reason) The function of history is to observe the past and understand the present, and to use the gains of past human life, academics, and ideas as the basis for improving today's human life and social undertakings. However, according to the curriculum standards, it seems to focus on the historical materials of political dynasties, so it is appropriate to compress the historical materials as much as possible and increase the historical materials of people's livelihood and the historical materials of academic thought. B. Lack of central thought. (Reason) Although the history curriculum is inevitable from the flat narrative of facts due to the times, there should be a central thought to connect all the materials. For example, the Three Principles of the People in modern China is the standard for unifying people's thoughts. The history curriculum may as well use the origin or evolution of the Three Principles of the People as a central thought, so that scholars can learn with a purpose, and the historical materials will not be scattered and have nowhere to go. (To be continued)

Free Talk

World Anecdotes 96

—Sea Traveler

The Metropolitan Museum of Art in New York City uses electricity to protect its displayed treasures. If someone moves an item, the entire museum immediately closes, and everyone inside is confined, unable to leave.

The largest aircraft currently in Britain can only carry twenty-two people. However, last year, several large aircraft were built in London that can carry forty people and have bar and smoking room facilities.

The banks of the Amazon River in South America produce many strange trees. One type of tree bark contains sweet juice that tastes like sugar. Another type of tree secretes oil that looks and smells like lard.

The city of Norwich in England breeds canaries, which is an important industry. Each season, as many as 100,000 birds are shipped out.

Russia is currently training a team of women, organized according to military law, who are trained to use rifles and machine guns to defend ammunition factories in times of war.

During a major storm in 1929, Scottish fishing boats lost 31,000 fishing nets. Replacements would cost 150,000 British pounds.

More Stories of Martial Arts 97

—Green Pine Hermit

Shaolin is known throughout the world for its boxing prowess. The so-called Inner School originated with Zhang Sanfeng of the Song Dynasty. Sanfeng was a Taoist from Wudang. He was alert and used stillness to control movement. He did not reveal his skills casually, and only acted when extremely necessary. When he did act, he was always accurate and effective, with every strike knocking his opponent down. After a hundred years, this technique was passed down, but few studied it. This skill is now like the lost music Guangling San. Today, martial arts are flourishing, and Commissioner Hu Pu'an of the Civil Affairs Department is vigorously promoting them. Perhaps the Inner School will be revived. I have gathered stories from elders about several practitioners of the Inner School. While I cannot vouch for the value of their techniques, they may be helpful.

In the old Chuansha, there was Lu Shaotao, who mastered the secret techniques of Zhang Sanfeng. He thoroughly understood the subtleties. One day, he went out at night to investigate something and was captured by guards, who tied him to a pillar. A dozen guards surrounded him. Shaotao picked up a piece of broken porcelain and secretly cut his bonds. He took out silver and threw it into the air. While the guards were scrambling for it, Shaotao escaped. The dozen guards chased him but fell to the ground, unable to get up. Later, he encountered several soldiers on the road who tried to draw their swords. Shaotao was quick and strong, striking their shoulders. The soldiers were thrown to the ground, their swords falling. Shaotao ran away, too fast to be caught.

Feng Guanxiong of Shandong was exceptionally brave and agile, and was called invincible. One day, a monk visited and asked to wrestle. The monk looked fierce and spoke arrogantly, saying, "If you can punch me once or kick me once, I will admit defeat. Otherwise, you are not a man." Feng watched him for a long time, concentrating and gathering his strength. As the monk raised his fist to strike, Feng kicked him in the shoulder. The monk hit a stone wall, which collapsed, and his arm broke. The monk left with his injury, no longer arrogant. Feng was skilled in Yi Jin Jing, which allowed him to kick with such force, causing both the monk and the wall to fall.

Zhang Zhiyi of Yunjian was wealthy. As a child, he was gentle and refined, lacking the air of a strong man. Local bullies often harassed him. Zhang was furious and wanted revenge. He went to a Shaolin temple and asked to become a disciple. The monk said, "You are a weak scholar. Why learn martial arts?" Zhang insisted, so the monk gave him an iron mallet and told him to throw it with the strength of both feet. He started with 50 pounds, then 100 pounds. After a year, he improved greatly. The monk then gave him a mallet weighing 300 pounds, which he played with like an iron ball, throwing it accurately and powerfully. The monk was pleased and said, "You have mastered the technique." Zhang then left the temple. The bullies saw him return and tried to harass him again. Zhang grabbed one of them in the crowd with both feet and threw him a hundred paces. The crowd panicked and tried to attack Zhang, but as soon as they approached, they were thrown. The bullies were scared and warned each other not to provoke him.

Rose Talk 98

—Chen Boying

The rose is a type of shrub, very similar to the rose. It is two or three feet tall, with thorns. The leaves are oval, the sepals are green, and the flower receptacle is cup-shaped. The flowers are purple, but some are white, though these are rare. The fragrance is strong. It flowers in early summer and grows everywhere, but the roses from Wuxing are especially abundant. When the flowers bloom, the villagers gather them and sell them in the city, filling baskets and hampers. The drug stores and temporary flower merchants in the city buy the flowers and dry them. The drying method involves spreading the flowers on a fine sieve and drying them over a charcoal fire. The heat must be just right; too little and they will be soft, too much and they will crumble. Only those experienced in this trade can judge it correctly. This lasts for about ten days and is called the "flower market." Once the flowers are dried, they are sold by the tens of thousands, worth dozens of silver dollars. They are used to make perfume, distilled water, wine, and sugar. According to elders, during the Qianlong era of the Qing Dynasty, there was a wealthy man in Wuxing named Song Haifan who liked to spend lavishly. He gathered roses and built a archway in his garden, three zhang high. The fragrance was intoxicating, and people flocked to see it. There was another man named Chen Wending, whose wealth was equal to Song's but who was competitive. He wanted to outdo Song and planned to build two archways to overshadow Song's. However, the flower market lasted only a few days, and despite his efforts, he could only gather half the number of flowers. Chen was furious and threw all the flowers under the Camel Bridge. For a time, the river water turned into purple clouds.

At the Leprosy Banquet 99

—Wu Yunmeng

Leprosy is not an incurable disease. If treated in a timely manner, it can be cured. People are unaware of this and consider it a chronic disease, which leads to delays and ultimately to incurable conditions. The disease is passed on to future generations, causing endless harm. Is this not lamentable? The Chinese Leprosy Relief Association is dedicated to leprosy relief with enthusiasm, painstaking effort, and unwavering dedication. It established the Hongkou Clinic first and then the Leprosy Hospital, benefiting the poor and bringing happiness to patients. Nothing can be added. Recently, Dr. Wade, a global leprosy expert, came from the Philippines. A trade delegation of overseas Chinese from the Dutch East Indies also came from overseas. The Leprosy Association hosted a banquet to welcome them. It was a grand occasion with many attendees, including Mr. Jordan, the Director of the Municipal Council Health Department, Dr. Patterson, the Director of Renji Hospital, Yan Fuqing, Diao Xinde, Zhu Shaoping, Li Yuanxin, and dozens of others. I learned many interesting things during the banquet.

The overseas Chinese trade delegation consisted of eighteen people, all prominent figures in the local community. I met Zhuang Xiyan, the deputy head of the delegation, and shook hands with him, reminiscing about the past. We had a long conversation. He was straightforward and honest, and expressed concern about the declining overseas trade. He also lamented the fluctuating exchange rates, which made it difficult to earn even a small profit. If this continues, the consequences are unimaginable. Therefore, this trip to China was intended to join hands with the domestic business community and work together for development. He also said that the natives of Java are increasingly fond of printed cloth, which sells well in the market, and reject local cloth like dirt. They only care about the bright colors and do not care about the quality. They wear new clothes for less than ten days before the colors fade and the clothes tear. They then discard them and buy new ones. The natives are so simple-minded that their extinction is not far off. His deep concern was evident in his words. During the banquet, I also sat next to Wu Wenjian, who owns a large rice mill and is a wealthy businessman. According to him, he is illiterate and uneducated, relying solely on his own efforts to succeed. He has lived in Java for over twenty years and has never heard of a Chinese delegation coming to investigate business opportunities. Countries like the United States, Japan, Germany, and France do this every year. What is their intention? It is obvious that they want to seize the foundation that our Chinese descendants have painstakingly built over hundreds of years and control our destiny. He is also a patriot with deep concern for the country.

As the banquet drew to a close, Chairman Li Yuanxin gave a welcoming speech. Dr. Wade stood up and gave a speech, saying that the leprosy cause owes its current achievements to the enthusiastic support of the community. Leprosy is curable, but the problem is that it is not treated promptly. Finally, Wu Zhijian, the secretary of the association, reported on the association's five-year plan, including convening a national leprosy conference, investigating the number of leprosy cases in China, and drafting leprosy laws. His most alarming statement was that there are 2 million leprosy patients worldwide, and China accounts for nearly half of them. These one million patients are constantly spreading the virus, passing it on to their children and grandchildren. If we do not take immediate action to eradicate it, the consequences are unimaginable. The speech was thought-provoking and moved the audience. By the time the banquet ended, it was already past ten o'clock.

Notes on Domino Grass 100

—Qing Qu

In my backyard, under an old wall, grows a small grass called domino grass. Every early summer, it sways green and lush. Although it is not as tall as a table, it shines among the mossy steps, far surpassing potted plants. Its shape resembles ferns, and the back of the leaves has tiny dots all over. At first glance, it looks like dominoes. Botanists say that it is a cryptogam, and the dots are cells that contain its seeds.

I have consulted Qian Tangzhao Shuxuan's "Supplement to the Compendium of Materia Medica," which mentions fish and turtle gold star grass. Fish grass has long, pointed leaves, while turtle grass has short, round leaves. This is their difference. The back of old fish grass leaves has gold stars, while turtle grass leaves do not, even when dry. The small gold star grass has leaves like duck feet, with dots on the back resembling the suits of dominoes, but five or six suits are missing. In the past, Yu Yinfu of Deqing called it seven-star grass, which probably refers to domino grass, as mentioned in his "Chunzaitang Collection." Whether or not this is true, I cannot say for sure.

When I was young, during breaks from studying, I often arranged this grass in pairs until there were no missing ones. Sometimes I used them to play "Five Passes." Otherwise, I would put them in my books. Over time, the green pigment in the leaves would gradually disappear, turning purplish-brown. They then looked even more like dominoes, and their smoothness resembled ivory. They were pleasing to the eye and enjoyable to play with, so I loved them very much. This grass still exists, but it is not easy to transplant. It is sensitive to sunlight and thrives in shady places surrounded by moss. It grows and multiplies between the courtyard steps, and the number of dots is always accurate.

Announcement: "Travels in India" has not yet been completed. It will continue after "Travels Around the Yellow River" is finished. Readers, please take note.

Travels Around the Yellow Sea (8) 101

—Huang Yanpei

The Shandong authorities asked us what we saw here. One gentleman replied that what we saw that was good was not as good as what we did not see. The listeners did not understand. He said, "We came to the factories and did not see labor unrest. We came to the schools and did not see student unrest. The workers are working peacefully, and the students are studying peacefully. This is a great thing. We hope that the authorities can maintain this situation for a long time. At the same time, we should take this opportunity to work hard and make progress, and not waste this good opportunity."

Li Junyi, the magistrate of Shenyang County, and Jin Jing'an, the secretary-general of the provincial government, guided us to a village north of the North Mausoleum called Da Hanying Village. It was very interesting. First, we visited a small school with 116 boys and 26 girls. The annual cost was 2,318 yuan. The school was built by the school director, Zheng Rongxi, who raised the funds. The village has 240 households and 1,232 people. Almost all school-age children are enrolled. There are 82 illiterate men and 50 illiterate women. There are no unemployed people. The statistics and charts in the village head's office were very informative. The four wealthiest families have over 300 mu of land and five or six mules. Most are tenant farmers. The main crops are sorghum, soybeans, and millet. There is very little wheat. There is no rice. The villagers have made their own rules, and those who deliberately steal or damage crops or livestock are punished accordingly.

We entered a Liu family's home. Five brothers were all married and had children, but they still lived together. The eldest brother was a cook, and the four younger brothers were all farmers. The house was only one row facing south. The east room was the bedroom for the eldest brother and his wife. The west room was large, with four kangs (platforms) facing each other. The four couples, with their children, each occupied one kang, publicly displaying the meaning of the poems "Husbands and wives are in harmony, and brothers are united." At the west end of the room was the ancestral tablet, where the whole family paid their respects on the first and fifteenth of each month. This showed the simplicity and sincerity of their customs, containing much of the ancient ways. Outside the door, the small courtyard was filled with livestock, carts, and farm products. The whole family was busy with their work.

The old name of this village was Hanying Village. There is a story. In the early Qing Dynasty, the father of Yan Xizhai (Yuan), named Chang, was abducted to Liaodong. He died and was buried in this village. This is mentioned in the chronicle of Yan Xizhai. Xizhai could not find his father's grave, so he summoned his soul and brought back his spirit tablet. Today, the grave cannot be found.

Farewell to Jin Jing'an, Yang Ziwo, and other friends in Shenyang.

At the Hai Dian Jingtuo, I weep with tears. At the Zhaoling, the carved beams are still proud. The mountains and rivers are desolate after a hundred battles. I feel lonely and alienated in the wind and rain. My hair is turning gray with sorrow. Spring comes slowly to the purple frontier. What can I say about the twenty years of Kangji (relief)? I am already jaded by the cry of the wild geese.

Book Spinning Association

Hawthorne's Detective Cases, Turning Point (19) 102

— Cheng Xiaoqing

Hawthorne's gaze was calm. He took two puffs of his cigarette and slowly nodded in agreement. "I also feel that way about her. However, the 'god of love' and the 'fairy of secrets' often have close relationships. Besides, since love comes from secrecy, we can't casually add the word 'trickery'. That being the case, let's assume someone is unilaterally in love with her, without Pei Fen being aware of it yet." I responded, "This assumption is quite plausible. However, once we talk about unilateral love, the scope is also quite broad. Could that person be her male classmate, or a relative, or a friend of Pei Xian? Where do we even start?" Hawthorne said, "It's indeed difficult to start, but it's not entirely without clues. For example, that necklace could also serve as a kind of clue." These words of his once again stirred up my previous doubts. I asked, "I still can't figure out this necklace issue. We've assumed that he misunderstood because of unrequited love, treating me as his rival in love, and therefore plotted to harm me. In that case, the necklace would be an important element in the assassination plan. But how could he have prepared it in such a short time? If you say he hid it in his pocket beforehand, specifically to make things difficult for me, that doesn't seem logical either. What do you think is the origin of this thing?" Hawthorne lowered his head again and threw the cigarette butt into the spittoon. Then he looked up, a faint smile playing on the corners of his lips. He slowly replied, "This is indeed a difficult question. As I see it, this thing was definitely not specially prepared for you. However, before explaining this doubt, we must first ascertain the truth about this person. What is this person's status? What is their character? All of these are relevant. For example, if he were a dissolute, romantic young man, then the counterfeit decorations on his body may not be limited to just one necklace. If he encounters an opportunity, he uses these fake goods as bait to deceive women. This is one way to understand it." I nodded and said, "There are indeed such young men everywhere. These people are truly the enemies of women, truly deserving of death!" Hawthorne gave a cold laugh and said, "Why do you have to make such pointless sentiments? These few grumbles of yours, will they have any impact on society?" I sighed and asked, "Don't you have a second ideal?" Hawthorne suddenly stood up, his face grave, and answered in a rather cold tone, "If this young man's behavior goes a step further than romantic, and his aim is not only the satisfaction of lust, but also focused on the issue of money, then the role of this necklace is even more terrible." I asked again, "Are you saying that he prepared this necklace in order to use his fraudulent means at any time, to exchange the fake for the real?" Hawthorne did not answer. He glanced at his watch and said hurriedly, "Oh, it's past one o'clock. We don't need to just talk anymore. Su Ma, hurry up and make food. I have things to do after eating."

Silk and Tea, Spring Cocoon Production in Hangzhou is Poor and of Inferior Quality 114

Cocoon production is less than 30%... Mostly Thin-Skinned Cocoons

This year, the early silkworms raised by farmers in the four villages of Hangzhou County all died completely during the first sleep due to the cold weather. The silkworm farmers re-hatched late silkworms, but the weather was still cold, and the silkworm ants changed from time to time. By the time of the big sleep and prosperous leaves, there was heavy rain for ten days and the severe cold was like winter, resulting in most of the silkworm ants suffering from vomiting and diarrhea, resulting in huge losses. The silkworms that went up to the cluster were still shrinking and lying dormant due to the strangely cold weather, strong winds and rain, and the silk production was insufficient. The new cocoons have now been listed, and the overall pull is less than three and a half years old, and the cocoon quality is inferior, with mostly thin-skinned double cocoons. Only two-tenths of the cocoon shops are operating. The high-quality cocoons open at 46 yuan, and each shop receives very little goods.

Wuyuan New Tea Opening Price Initial Sound 117

New tea in Wuyuan, after each shop dispatched partners to the village to search for purchases, there were rumors of approaching negotiations every day, but the price was tight. Xin tea, known as the best water leaves, was priced at 55 yuan to 50 yuan per dan by each shop, which was a far cry from the previous year's price of 80 to 72 yuan, and many were unwilling to sell it cheaply. Today, Yintai in Beixiang opened the scale by the village Tongqing, setting the price at 40 yuan per dan, which is half the price of last year's high price. In the afternoon, Liujiaxia was opened by Xigu Gong, and the pricing was the same as Yintai. This is the vanguard of Wuyuan tea's opening price this year. The shops heard the news and recognized that the price was fair, and both parties wanted to handle it at this price. It is expected that the villages that have finished harvesting new tea will continue to open the price in the next few days. The new tea in Gaobo, which is connected to the border of Wuyuan, has been harvested and produced by each household, and the shipment is also more tender than last year. Although a few local tea shops have been trying to open the market, the actual financial exhaustion after the bandits prevents them from increasing their appetite, and the tea market has become oversupplied. Yesterday, Wucheng Hengda Li Tea Shop had already opened a sporadic selection of scales in the new building, setting the price at 30 yuan per dan, which was 20 yuan lower than the old price. Other shops also priced within this range. The shops had a stalemate for a while.

Qiupu Tea Market is Depressed 118

Qiupu has always been an important area for the production of black tea. In the 16th and 17th years of the Republic of China, there were more than 40 foreign tea shops operating. Since the sluggish overseas sales in the previous year, most of the tea shops have suffered losses. Last year, they suffered heavy losses again. Therefore, those with weak capital are unable to seek a resurgence, and those with thick capital hold a negative attitude. This year, the number of tea shops opening in Taoshu Shop, where the tea market is concentrated, has been reduced by half compared with the previous year, and other places are also rare. However, the mountain price this year has not fallen due to the increase in Qifu. The opening price of new tea is between 70 and 30 yuan, among which, the output of Fenliu, Xianglinwan, Yipinjian, and Yingxi is abundant and the sales volume is large. The other low-quality teas are rarely asked about. Each shop, in view of the sluggish Shanghai market and the abundant stock of British line tea, does not dare to import too much, and each holds the purpose of doing less is better. The trend of the tea market is becoming increasingly depressed.

Wu Tiecheng Visits Sun Ke 122

Zhang Ji Will Go to Guangdong in a Few Days

Sun Ke Will Not Return to Nanjing for the Time Being

Central Committee member Wu Tiecheng arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday morning and went to visit Minister of Railways Sun Ke at Dian Li Ai Road at 3:30 pm to discuss the Guangdong issue and a peaceful solution. He left at 5 pm. After Sun Ke and Wu Tiecheng met, our reporter specially visited Wu to inquire about the Guangdong affair and whether there were any concrete results in the consultation. Wu replied to the reporter that the Guangdong issue is still under discussion, and Minister Sun will not return to Nanjing for the time being, but has agreed to telegraph the Guangdong side again. The reporter then asked whether Mr. Wu would go to Guangdong. Wu replied that he would not go, and the Central Government is now sending Mr. Zhang Puquan to Guangdong. Mr. Zhang is ill in Nanjing, but is expected to leave in a day or two. The reporter then asked about the Central Government's attitude towards Mr. Hu Hanmin. Wu replied that Mr. Hu himself hopes to go abroad, while the Central Government hopes that Mr. Hu will stay in Nanjing and jointly take responsibility for the party and the country. Hu has not yet made a concrete statement on this. As for the issue of Hu's whereabouts, the Nanjing side has not raised it. Wu finally told reporters that the report that the Guangdong side has a plan to organize a military government, hoping that it will not become a reality, otherwise it will cause difficulties in mediation. Now that the National Assembly has been successful, all the construction of the tutelage period depends on peaceful unification. It is deeply hoped that the whole country will unanimously support peaceful unification at this critical moment.

The Special City Party Department sent a telegram to Chen Jitang yesterday, (the title is omitted) The founding of the Republic of China was difficult and arduous.
