Preparation for the Road and City Exhibition 179

— Wu Fei

The China National Road Construction Association has been established for ten years since its founding in the Republic of China. Therefore, the authorities of the association have organized a road and city exhibition to commemorate the tenth anniversary. It was originally scheduled to be held in April of this year. However, due to the time-consuming manufacturing, sending, and displaying of exhibits from remote provinces and foreign countries, the 16th Executive Committee meeting decided to postpone it and officially open it before August to September 12, so that all regions can prepare in a leisurely manner. The Road Exhibition can be opened with complete items to enhance the spectacle. The association has submitted a request to the Executive Yuan to order its subordinates to actively rush to manufacture the required exhibits. On the one hand, it also sent letters to the Ministry of Railways, Ministry of Interior, Ministry of Transportation, and Ministry of Industry to check. It also sent letters to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to telegraph to the embassies and consulates abroad to ask the road and city authorities and factories in each country to send personnel to participate and transport the exhibits to China to broaden their knowledge. The method of soliciting exhibits is to take exquisite pictures of 12 inches or more of the completed work and ongoing projects within the scope of road and city transportation. Such as newly built roads, bridges, and parks in historical sites, new buildings of all sizes, and new inventions for road construction, road maintenance, and transportation machinery, vehicles, oil tankers, etc., must be accompanied by detailed Chinese and Western instructions. Glue photos and models to the top of each vehicle and machine exhibit for the record or photography of Chinese and foreign representatives and Chinese and foreign people to take back to their respective countries and provinces and cities for display and permanent commemoration. On the one hand, the association will compile and print a special issue of the exhibition to promote it and provide a reference. Therefore, this year's Road and City Memorial Exhibition of the Road Association brings together the achievements of road and city transportation at home and abroad. It is an unprecedented international road and city exhibition. The work achievements, charts, and models will be designed and refined separately in the future and must be sent to the meeting one month before the opening for easy arrangement and decoration to enhance the spectacle and provide comparison. The domestic road and city exhibits outline planned by the association is as follows:

(A) Name distinction (1) The Capital Road and City Exhibition Hall focuses on the specific design of the capital's road and city government, the existing achievements, and the municipality's library's exquisitely made models, charts, statistics, etc. (2) The Jiangsu Road and City Exhibition Hall focuses on the specific plans of the Jiangsu trunk and branch roads, the past and present achievements, and the models and charts of Suzhou City, etc. (3) The Shanghai Road and City Exhibition Hall focuses on the design of Greater Shanghai and the current construction achievements of the municipal government, as well as exquisitely made books, tables, photos, and models, and fire protection and hygiene exhibits, etc. (4) The Zhejiang Road and City Exhibition Hall pays attention to the Hangzhou municipal administration and the construction achievements of trunk and branch roads in the province, as well as the specific plans for road and city transportation in the province, fire protection and hygiene exhibits, etc. (5) The Hubei Road and City Exhibition Hall focuses on the construction achievements of the Hankou municipal administration and the trunk and branch roads in the province. (6) The Hebei Road and City Exhibition Hall focuses on the construction achievements of the Beiping and Tianjin municipal administrations and the trunk and branch roads in the province. (7) The Guangdong Road and City Exhibition Hall focuses on the construction achievements of the Guangzhou municipal administration and the trunk and branch roads in the province. (8) The Liaoning Road and City Exhibition Hall focuses on the construction achievements of the Shenyang municipal administration and the self-run railway and road trunk and branch lines in the province. (9) The Sichuan Road and City Exhibition Hall focuses on the current construction achievements and specific designs of the Chengdu and Chongqing municipal administrations and the trunk and branch roads in the province. (10) The Guizhou Road and City Exhibition Hall focuses on the achievements and specific designs of the Guiyang municipal administration and the more than 5,000 miles of completed trunk and branch roads and bridges and culverts in the province. (11) Other provincial road and city exhibition halls. (B) Summary of exhibits (The following are the main exhibits required for the above-mentioned road and city exhibition halls) (1) Detailed design full map of the trunk and branch roads of each province and city, indicating the Chinese and English descriptions of the completed and uncompleted areas, and the symbols of the completed and uncompleted areas. (2) Photos or models of completed works of roads and bridges in each province and city, especially those with original historical sites. (3) In addition to the exquisitely made overall design models, charts, and instructions, each city government must also send the construction achievements of all agencies under the city government to the meeting for review and separate display in exquisitely made charts, photos, and models. (4) Special large buildings of road and city agencies in each province, such as the rugged and dangerous areas of Sichuan, Guizhou, and Guangxi, become wide and flat roads, and the large iron bridge over the Pearl River in Guangzhou. Henan and Shaanxi dug hundreds of miles of towering mountains and ridges from Hangu Pass to Tongguan, and became a 60-foot wide and flat automobile avenue. The design of the Huangpu Port Bridge, etc., should be specially made with illustrations and models to highlight the great construction projects in our country that are extremely difficult and dangerous, and encourage provinces, cities, districts, and counties that have not yet actively engaged in construction. (5) If there are new inventions of automobiles, electric vehicles, gasoline tires, wheels, and machines for road construction and road maintenance, and materials required for road and city construction in each province, city, and county, the specimens, drawings, and original parts of vehicles, machines, wheels, and oil should be notified to the association in advance so that the exhibition hall site can be prepared and displayed separately at that time. (6) If the models, charts, photos, vehicle machines, and objects exhibited by each province and city are damaged or dirty during long-distance transportation to Shanghai and cannot be repaired, they will not be displayed. (7) The exhibits of each province and city will not be displayed if they are found to be of poor quality, erroneous, or inconsistent in the examination and inspection of the committee. (8) If the exquisite exhibits of each province and city reach more than 100 pieces, a special site for the road and city exhibition hall of a certain province should be established, with an area of ​​a certain amount. The rent to be paid should be specially reduced by half compared to the rent for foreign exhibits to show preferential treatment. If there are no exquisitely made road and city models and special design charts, photos, etc., a road and city exhibition hall of a certain province or city will not be specially set up. The incoming items will only be displayed separately in the public hall, and the names of each province, city, county, and city will still be marked. (9) The cost of decoration, electric lights, scenery, flowers, glass frames, and watchmen in each provincial road and city exhibition hall must be paid by the representatives specially sent by each province and city to the meeting in accordance with the actual number used and officially signed and collected by the association. The representatives will report the expenses to their respective competent agencies. (10) Each exhibition hall must prepare at least 300 yuan for decoration and watchmen's expenses. Those with large pieces occupying a wide area must increase the expenses. Please notify the association before July of the number of exhibits and the area to be occupied so that the site can be prepared. At that time, it can still be compared with the exhibition halls of the UK, the US, Germany, and France that have joined the association.

Page 18

It is reported that the governments of the United Kingdom and the United States have agreed to donate 20,000 to 30,000 yuan for the decoration expenses of the exhibits of each country. Therefore, it is specially informed and hoped that a large number of charts and models will be actively and exquisitely made and delivered to the association in advance to rush to match the glass frames and wonderful scenery lights to enhance international glory and promote the great achievements of road and city construction in each province. (11) The association will respond to the trend of the times and specially promote domestic products, expand sales channels, and recover rights and interests. If there are precious native products, raw material specimens, drawings, or exquisitely made objects in each province, city, and county, the representatives sent by each province can bring them to the meeting for display. However, each province shall not exceed 100 pieces at most, and the weight of each sample shall not exceed one jin. If it is a new invention of transportation and construction necessary vehicle machine materials, etc., this is not an exception.

The First Section of the Zhenju Road is Completed 180

— Jing Wu

The Zhenjiang-Jurong Highway is the main line of the Beijing-Hangzhou line to the capital of Jiangsu Province. It is 40 kilometers long in total. The first section, from Zhenjiang to Huifeng Temple, is about seven kilometers long. It has been completed and opened to traffic on a trial basis. The road is built with the latest methods. The stone surface is about four meters wide, and the construction is quite solid. The project is divided into about six parts. (1) Open the roadbed. (2) Lay large stones. (3) Lay small stones. (4) Pour mud. (5) Lay small gravel. (6) Lay fine sand. The road surface engineering is so refined that it is inferior to the Zhongshan Road in the provincial capital. It can be used for five or six years without repair. Moreover, the turning points are built in imitation of the railway construction method, with one side raised high so that the passenger does not feel the turning. Even driving fast is not a problem. Trees are planted on both sides of the road, mostly French parasol trees. Huifeng Temple is located at the junction of Wuzhou Mountain and Shili Changshan. The road turns around in the mountain, and the car travels in it. The two peaks are lined with trees, and the foot of the two mountains is covered with lush pines and the water seeps through the streams. The scenery is better than Zhaoyin. The car speed can be 40 to 50 yards. It is now planned to build three thatched cottages behind Huifeng Temple for summer vacation and medical treatment. The area along the road will soon be prosperous. The sections from Huifeng Temple to Jurong are also being actively prepared and constructed. The completion date will not be far away.

Random Chat About New Cars 181

— (Fu)

Characteristics of Dodge's New Car: The Dodge Eight-Cylinder New Car is a successful masterpiece meticulously structured by the great engineering experts of the Dodge Motor Company, who gathered their minds and exhausted their thoughts. The novelty of the design, the thoroughness of the planning, the ingenuity of the construction, and the excellence of the materials used are all outstanding and appropriate. The entire body, from the front bumper to the taillights, is low, even, symmetrical, exquisite, and ingenious. At a glance, it is known to be the latest style in terms of car bodies. Coupled with beautiful lines and harmonious colors, it feels even more pleasing to the eye, attracting people. The new-style water tank head, automatic water tank cover, and naturally curved front fenders are extremely soft and beautiful. The low, long hood, nickel screen, and outwardly extending windshield with a permanently installed sight glass are also notable. Needless to say, the car body is made of a whole piece of steel, and all the major parts are integrated as if seamlessly woven. It is appropriate that it is strong, excellent, and extremely safe. As for spaciousness, steadiness, and quietness, it cannot be compared to ordinary vehicles. The front seats are easy to adjust, so they are suitable for all body types, allowing for extreme comfort. The interior of the sedan also has armrests and support straps. The ashtray is placed on the rear door. The clothes rack, corner lights, dome light, etc., are all complete. The dashboard and all decorative strips are constructed with high-grade wood and exquisite craftsmanship. The interior hardware is all nickel, and the exterior hardware is completely plated with nickel, making it incomparably shiny and dazzling. Various special superior cushions and matching colors are available for selection, each according to preference, all extremely appropriate. The wheelbase is lengthened to one hundred and eighteen inches. The newly invented dual-core low-grid frame reduces the overall height by four inches, and the ground clearance does not feel reduced. Being in the car allows for free movement and is extremely comfortable. The engine construction is particularly superior, and the mechanical power is exceptionally substantial. The piston displacement is two hundred forty and three hundred thirty cubic inches. The bore and stroke are three inches X four and one-quarter inches. At three thousand two hundred revolutions per minute, the power is eighty-four horsepower. The entire rubber insulation method is adopted, so there is no concern about shocks or tremors even when driving on rough roads. The famous internal expansion type wheel hydraulic brake is convenient to manage and has a great effect. Regardless of the speed of the car or the quality of the road, it is always easy to handle and control freely. All of these are the major features of the Dodge new car. If the rest of the small parts have undergone continuous improvements and are becoming more and more beautiful, it is enough to give buyers extreme satisfaction.

Chevrolet's New Car Arrives in Shanghai: Since the new 1931 Chevrolet car was launched last November, it has gained unprecedented acclaim in the American automotive industry. Now, its first batch of new cars to be shipped to China has arrived in Shanghai and will be displayed at the Jardine Matheson Building at 456 Avenue Foch from May 8 for a public exhibition.

According to Mr. He Zhenbo Xu, the owner of Jardine Matheson, this new 1931 Chevrolet set a new record in world car sales in December last year and January and February of this year. Its sales ratio accounts for 33.5% of all types of vehicles worldwide. Therefore, although the General Motors factory can manufacture 70,000 Chevrolets per month, the demand exceeds the supply, and the shortage is still significant. Even overseas distributors can only seek one or two vehicles for display purposes and cannot obtain them. Although General Motors has exhausted its efforts to rush production, it is still not enough to meet the domestic demand in the United States.

Speaking of the new Chevrolet car itself, it has the characteristics of various high-priced cars. The arc angles of the entire car and its lengthened 109-inch wheelbase are properly matched, making the appearance of the entire car more beautiful. The water tank has also been transformed, and the headlights are arranged in parallel on a specially made crossbar. All exposed metal parts of the front of the car are chrome-plated, making them dazzling and reflective.

The rear window of the new Chevrolet is specially widened, forming an extremely dignified appearance with its beautiful body. The front window is the famous Fei Xian VV type glass, which is clean and clear and has no concern about glare.

The dashboard inside the car has a speedometer, oil pressure gauge, temperature gauge, gasoline gauge, electric lock, carburetor choke, light switch, spark lever, and throttle knob, etc. The various instruments are appropriately arranged and illuminated with reflected light, making them even more obvious.

The new-style three-spoke steering wheel is constructed with precise calculations. It is made of pressed steel and protected by a rubber sleeve, so its movements are agile, strong, and reliable.

The padding inside the car body is made of beautiful woven fabrics, and the seats are suitable for the human body. In the special sedan, there are armrests, ribbons, and double smoking seats. The driver's seats of all sedans can be freely adjusted to fit the driver's height and habits.

Regarding the mechanical aspects of the new Chevrolet, in addition to the powerful engine, its manifold can sense heat extremely strongly, so its starting is sensitive. The cast iron of its cylinders is carefully sealed and cooled in a timely manner, and it can generate the strongest power at low speeds. This greatly increases the power for extending the life of the vehicle. The front end of the crankshaft is equipped with a special tuner. In addition, there are cleaners, shock absorbers, ventilators, and accelerator pumps, etc., with the latest automotive equipment. The forty-eight-pound heavy crankshaft and its large oil surface bearings are only seen in cars.

The steel teeth of the flywheel are smooth and clean and fit closely with the gears of the starting motor. In this way, countless starting difficulties can be avoided and the service life can be increased.

When it is in use, this new Chevrolet will surprise you with its unique advantages. Its smooth power, comfortable driving, agile acceleration, and free operation all demonstrate its soaring progress and have truly entered the ranks of the highest-grade cars.

With a speed of seventy miles per hour and the above features, it is a special contribution to the automotive industry in recent years. Do you still have any doubts?

One Thousand Mile Car Race: The car race held in Italy the other day had a course of one thousand miles. The number of participating vehicles was as many as one hundred, which stirred up the whole of Europe and was extremely grand. It is indeed worthy of being the first major sports event of the year related to international honor. At the same time, it is also one of the important long-distance races. As a result of the competition, Mr. Carlo Schell won the victory trophy amidst cheers. The car he was driving was a new 1931 sports car from the German Benz Motor Company. All the participants this time were the best of the time, and the vehicles they rode were all excellent and outstanding. It is appropriate that the competition was fierce, and the final victory was absolutely not accidental. It can be imagined.

The competition site is in the city of Brescia in Italy. It is planned to depart from this place, pass through Bologna and Florence, and arrive in Rome. Then from Rome to Ancona on the Adriatic River, then Bologna, then Verona, then Padua, and then turn back to the starting point, the city of Brescia. The total distance traveled reached 1,022 miles. Even a long-distance race is no more than this. What is even more noteworthy is that part of the route is rugged and bad, making it difficult to travel. Part of it is mountainous, winding and tortuous, making it difficult to drive fast. Some say that this kind of competition is truly no different from the most difficult and rigorous test of people and vehicles. If the driver is not proficient in driving, he will not be able to quickly and successfully complete the task. If the car he drives is not of superior quality and well-made, it is not enough to talk about the competition.

There were 103 vehicles participating in the competition, of all sizes and styles, produced in various countries. However, only Mr. Carlo Schell joined the competition from Germany to compete with Italian and other national players. And the final victory also belongs to Mr. Carlo. This has to be attributed to the high speed and absolute reliability of the SSK Benz car he drives. He finished the race in sixteen hours and ten minutes, always in the lead. The average speed was sixty-three miles per hour, which was much earlier than the second-place car, the Romeo car driven by the Italian player Campari. After the results were announced, not only the Germans were proud of it, but also all countries in Europe were surprised and envious and praised it.

World Car Scraps 183

— Pei

Chrysler's Heavy Responsibility and Far-Reaching Achievements: The Chrysler Motor Company deserves to receive letters of praise from users of the car, saying that the car is durable, long-lasting, and far-reaching. There was a 1924 Chrysler sedan that has traveled 20,000 miles and can still be used on the road and still has the hope of winning a competition. There is another Chrysler car, which the owner bought in 1925, and its mileage has reached 183,000 miles.

Ms. Frey Wins the Championship: Mildred Frey, a girl from Milwaukee, won the world championship for endurance in car driving. Ms. Diefley defeated Ms. Naisher Lee's record in Indianapolis with a persistence of 120 hours. Frey was driving a Desa Tor six-cylinder car, which had 45 hours more endurance than Naisher Lee. The location for driving the car was Fei Xia Park in Milwaukee. It is said that Ms. Frey's car driving record is unmatched by any woman in the world.

Brazil Builds National Roads: The Brazilian government is now planning to build car roads that pass through the whole country. A committee on this plan has now been established to consider this construction so that it can be implemented. According to the original plan, the new roads will connect the roads of various states to each other.

One-Tenth Engaged in the Automotive Industry: The British automotive industry is well-developed in the world. According to the California Automobile Association, in the United States of America, one out of ten people must be engaged in the automotive industry. However, their work is initially not fixed. It may be manufacturing, sales, investment, or service, only the difference between direct and indirect.

Loudspeaker Used on Cars: In the British automotive industry, there is a new invention of car equipment, which is a loudspeaker. This loudspeaker is installed next to the steering wheel. When driving, the driver can issue a loud warning signal to alert pedestrians far away, or he can expand the opinions in the driver's mind and tell the police to ensure the safety of the car.

Business News 184

The Qitian Stage declares that since this stage caters to social psychology and has produced a great stage design and interspersed with the novel and special Fan Lihua moving mountains and overturning seas, it has been packed day and night, even so crowded that it is impenetrable. Before the opening, customers gather like a tide, which is a phenomenon rarely seen in the Shanghai theatrical world in recent years. As for the play's composition, it is novel and different from the others, the plot is compact, and there is not a single dull scene. There are as many as seven or eight song and dance scenes, each extremely wonderful, interspersed and changed every day and night, without any repetition. Let's describe the outline of a few great scenes. The first scene is the military march in the mountains, which is mighty and magnificent. The three armies sing military songs, which resonate throughout the sky. The Xue family generals, in glorious military attire, with flags covering the sky, are all specially made. Even if the old novels describe them in detail, they still cannot describe one ten-thousandth of their appearance. Secondly, there is the Lishan Blessed Land, with jade-lettered towers, strange flowers and exotic plants, covering the cliffs. The immortals float in the blue waves, playing the Neon Clothes Song between the Orchid Pavilions. Fan Lihua, with her cloud-like hair, slowly descends from the auspicious clouds, dancing her most satisfying swordsmanship, named Haiyan Heqing. It was taught by a famous swordsman when Ms. Lu performed in Guangdong. Every rise and fall, every advance and retreat, has a solution, which is different from the ordinary. Moreover, it has been praised by internal experts many times. The Lishan Old Mother enlightens the future in the midst of green pines and cypresses, revealing the secrets of heaven, making people want to escape from the dust and forget the mundane. The third is moving mountains. Thousands of valleys and cliffs fly in the air. The lush and verdant boulders instantly surround Ding Shan like an iron bucket. The woodcutter on the top of the mountain lets down a rope to save him. Ding Shan climbs up the rope, but unexpectedly, the old woodcutter actually pulls out his short ladder, putting a brave general in a situation where he cannot go to heaven or earth. Mischievous squirrels even come to tease him. Do you think it is dangerous or not? Let's talk about the scene of overturning the sea. Thousands of acres of waves stand upright. The fish, turtles, snails, and clams at the bottom of the sea cannot settle down and dance and beg for mercy on the beach. Ding Shan floats and sinks on the sea surface, really wanting the audience to be anxious. The Xue Fan bridal chamber is the most beautiful plot in the whole play. The scene is graceful and luxurious, even more so than the palace. A good marriage turns into a bad marriage. Lihua is ambushed and goes to Lishan, knocking on the old mother to ask for the future result. This scene has wonderful changes and is extremely mysterious. The last scene is the evil spirits in Qinglong Pass. Ding Shan is surrounded in the fiery flames. Real fire fills the stage, and red dragons fly around, rushing straight towards Ding Shan. At this point, the audience wants to sweat for Ding Shan. Although the general is proud and brave, he has to call Lihua to save his life. The whole play then comes to an end. It can be said that it is the first-class work in this play, and so on.

Medical News 185

The pediatric expert Ren Nongxuan declares that Dr. Ren is good at treating children's fever and cough, shortness of breath and excessive phlegm, vomiting and diarrhea, measles and convulsions, as well as women's prenatal and postnatal problems and irregular menstruation, etc. He is rich in experience. He has been practicing medicine in Shanghai for more than 20 years. Now, because the weather is suddenly cold and hot, and diseases are prevalent, the general illnesses of infants, such as fever, cough, choking, measles, diarrhea, etc., arise in response to the season. Dr. Ren is a specialist in this disease, so many people come to him for treatment. The clinic has now moved to No. 229 Baoshun Lane, at the end of Beixiangfen Lane on the east side of Zhejiang Road, on Yingda Road, diagonally opposite the Great Shanghai Hotel, and so on.
